**Task:** Validate XPL‑USDT for a new short entry.

**Required checks:**
1. **Open‑position check** – confirm there is no existing position for XPL‑USDT.

**Available tools to perform checks:**
- `blofin_assess_portfolio` – returns blocked symbols and overall portfolio status.  
- `blofin_get_positions` – list current open positions (filter by `inst_id="XPL-USDT"`).  
- `blofin_rank_opportunities` (or `blofin_get_trade_insights`) – can provide recent 24h change/momentum data for a symbol; set `side="short"` and `top_n` high enough to include XPL‑USDT.  

**Next step:** Invoke the appropriate functions (e.g., `blofin_assess_portfolio`, `blofin_get_positions`, and `blofin_rank_opportunities` with `side="short"` or a similar query) to retrieve the needed data, then confirm whether XPL‑USDT satisfies all three conditions.

**Portfolio Assessment Summary**

| Symbol | Side | Qty | Avg. Price | Mark Price | Unrealized PnL | Status |
|--------|------|-----|-----------|------------|----------------|--------|
| **NOM‑USDT** | Long | 9 | 0.0016400 | 0.0016375 | **‑0.000228  (‑0.14 %)** | Open, **blocked for new BUYs**, missing TP/SL |
| **Q‑USDT** | Short | –1 | 0.0171360 | 0.0172895 | **‑0.015353  (‑0.90 %)** | Open, **blocked for new SELLs**, missing TP/SL |
| **PUMP‑USDT** | Short | –6 | 0.0015020 | 0.0014423 | **+0.358264  (+39.9 %)** | Open, **blocked for new SELLs**, missing TP/SL |

**Key Points**

1. **Open Positions:** 3 positions total, all currently **missing TP/SL** (`positions_missing_tpsl` includes every open symbol).  
2. **Blocked Symbols:**  
   - `NOM‑USDT` cannot receive any **new buy** orders.  
   - `Q‑USDT` and `PUMP‑USDT` cannot receive any **new sell/short‑add** orders.  
3. **Performance:**  
   - `PUMP‑USDT` is the only profitable position (+39.9 %).  
   - `NOM‑USDT` and `Q‑USDT` are small losers (‑0.14 % and ‑0.90 % respectively).  
4. **Compliance Rules:**  
   - No new orders may be placed on blocked symbols.  
   - Every open position **must** have a TP/SL; the system should call `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl` (or `blofin_place_tpsl`) to set a **wide TP** (≥5 % target) and a **tight SL** (≈1 %).  

**Immediate Action Required**

- **Fix missing TP/SL** for all three positions using `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`.  
- After TP/SL are in place, evaluate whether any position should be exited early (only if SL is hit).  
- Scan the broader market for a new candidate symbol that is **not blocked** and shows explosive 24‑h movement with real volume, then prepare a trade with the asymmetric‑payoff parameters (target 5‑10 %+, stop ≈1 %).  

**Errors / Issues**

- **All open positions lack TP/SL** – this violates the portfolio rule and leaves the account exposed.  
- No new trade can be placed this cycle because every potential candidate is currently blocked; the system must either **repair TP/SL first** or **skip trading** until an unblocked opportunity appears.  

---  

**Next Steps (per doctrine)**  

1. Call `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl` for `NOM‑USDT`, `Q‑USDT`, and `PUMP‑USDT` (set TP ≈5 % above entry for longs, ≈5‑10 % below entry for shorts; SL ≈1 % from entry).  
2. Re‑assess the portfolio after TP/SL are applied.  
3. If margin permits, search for a new, unblocked symbol with a large recent move and place a trade with the asymmetric‑payoff setup.
